```
function getPlanName(planId: string): string {
  if (!planId) return "WhatsApp Pro";
  const p = planId.toLowerCase();
  if (p.includes("premium"))       return "WhatsApp Premium";
  if (p.includes("all_in_one") || p.includes("ultimate")) return "GAP Ultimate Ecosystem";
  return "WhatsApp Pro";
}
```

```
frontend\src\App.jsx:6:import Contacts from './pages/Contacts'
frontend\src\App.jsx:7:import WhatsAppConnect from './pages/WhatsAppConnect'
frontend\src\App.jsx:8:import FlowBuilder from './pages/FlowBuilder'

frontend\src\App.jsx:46:              <Route path="/signup" eleme
...(truncated)
```

</details>

**Short Answer**

Haan, pricing banane se pehle sabse important decision yeh hai: tum user se **platform subscription** charge karoge, aur WhatsApp/Meta message cost ko **separate pass-through recharge/wallet** rakhoge. AiSensy bhi basically yehi karta hai: monthly SaaS fee + template/message charges alag.

Maine project mein dekha ki abhi billing already 3 plans par hai: Free, WhatsApp Pro ₹1599/mo, WhatsApp Premium ₹2999/mo in [BillingPage.jsx](c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/BillingPage.jsx:12), aur Razorpay payment link flow bhi hai in [create-whatsapp-payment-link](c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/supabase/functions/create-whatsapp-payment-link/index.ts:11). Lekin backend Baileys/QR-session based hai, official Cloud API nahi, dependency yahan hai: [backend/package.json](c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/package.json:15). Isliye pricing aur promises carefully likhne honge.

**AiSensy Pricing Ka Matlab**

AiSensy ka model:

- **Free Forever**: entry plan, small limits, lead capture.
- **Basic ₹1500/mo**: essential WhatsApp API + broadcast + live chat + agents.
- **Pro ₹3200/mo**: scheduler, analytics, tags/attributes, APIs, better automation.
- **Enterprise custom**: high volume, webhooks, priority support, higher speed.
- **Template/message charges extra**: marketing, utility, authentication message ka Meta cost separate.

Meta ke current official pricing page ke hisaab se WhatsApp Business Platform per delivered message charge karta hai, category aur recipient country ke basis par. Categories: marketing, utility, authentication, service. Service messages free hain, aur 24-hour customer service window mein user ko reply karna free hota hai. Click-to-WhatsApp ad/Page CTA se entry aaye to 72 hours tak messages free ho sakte hain. Source: WhatsApp Business Platform pricing page: https://whatsappbusiness.com/products/platform-pricing/

**Tumhare Product Ke Liye Recommended Pricing**

Mere hisaab se pehla version yeh rakho:

| Plan | Price | Best For | Limits / Features |
|---|---:|---|---|
| Free | ₹0 | Trial/testing | 1 WhatsApp number, 200 contacts, 1 agent, 2 flows, live chat, no bulk broadcast |
| Starter | ₹999/mo | Small shops | 1 number, 1,000 contacts, 1 agent, 5 flows, basic bot, manual broadcast |
| Growth | ₹1,999/mo | Active businesses | 1 number, 5 agents, 10,000 contacts, unlimited flows, broadcasts, tags, templates, basic analytics |
| Pro | ₹3,499/mo | Marketing + support teams | 2 numbers, 10 agents, advanced flow builder, campaign scheduler, AI bot, reports, integrations |
| Enterprise | Custom | High volume | Multi-number, SLA, webhooks/API, dedicated support, custom limits |

Add-ons:

- Extra WhatsApp number: ₹499-₹999/mo
- Extra agent: ₹299-₹499/mo
- AI bot/knowledge base: ₹999/mo or usage based
- Extra storage/media: usage based
- Done-for-you setup: ₹2,999-₹9,999 one-time
- Official API migration/setup: custom onboarding fee
- Message wallet/recharge: Meta charges + markup, for example 10-20%

**Billing Model Best Rahega**

Use this structure:

1. **Platform subscription**
   - Monthly / quarterly / yearly.
   - Yearly par 15-20% discount.
   - Features, agents, contacts, flows, analytics limits yahan control hon.

2. **Message wallet**
   - User recharge kare: ₹500 / ₹1000 / ₹5000.
   - Marketing/utility/authentication template delivered hone par wallet se deduct.
   - Service messages free/zero cost show karo.
   - Very important: “Meta/WhatsApp charges may change” disclaimer rakho.

3. **Usage overage**
   - Contact limit cross ho to upgrade prompt.
   - Agents/number add-on charge.
   - High broadcast volume par anti-spam guardrails.

**Sabse Badi Future Problems**

1. **Official API vs Baileys risk**
   Abhi project Baileys use kar raha hai, jo WhatsApp Web style automation hai. Is par “Official WhatsApp Business API” promise karna risky hoga. Agar tum AiSensy-type market mein compete karna chahte ho, long-term official Meta Cloud API path banana better hai.

2. **“Unlimited bulk messaging” dangerous hai**
   Current UI mein Pro features mein “Unlimited bulk messaging” hai. Yeh compliance aur abuse risk create karega. Better wording: “Broadcast campaigns with fair-use limits.” WhatsApp quality rating, blocks, spam reports future issue ban sakte hain.

3. **Meta pricing change hoti rahegi**
   Meta ne pricing model already per-message direction mein shift kiya hai. Agar tum fixed bundle mein messages include kar doge, margin loss ho sakta hai. Isliye message cost ko wallet/pass-through rakho.

4. **Current payment is payment-link, true subscription nahi**
   Razorpay payment link one-time payment jaisa hai. Subscription renewals, expiry, grace period, invoice, failed payment, cancellation, upgrade/downgrade logic abhi mature nahi lagta. `expires_at`, `current_period_end`, `subscription_status`, `plan_limits` required honge.

5. **Feature limits enforce nahi hue to revenue leak hoga**
   Billing page par plans hain, but backend/API level par limits enforce karna zaroori hai: contacts count, flows count, agents count, broadcasts/day, numbers/account.

6. **GST/invoice/refund clarity**
   India mein pricing page par “+ GST” clearly mention karo. Refund policy, failed payment, prepaid wallet refund rules bhi define karo.

Meri recommendation: pehle **Growth ₹1,999/mo** ko main plan banao, **Pro ₹3,499/mo** ko serious businesses ke liye rakho, aur message charges ko subscription mein include mat karo. AiSensy jaise structure ko copy kar sakte ho, but tumhare project ke current architecture ke hisaab se “Official API” promise tabhi karo jab Meta Cloud API integration real ho.

## Codex <sup>6/9/2026, 1:53:59 PM</sup>

Bilkul. Main isko phases mein tod raha hoon so implementation ke time koi task miss na ho. Core idea yeh rahega:

**Subscription = platform access**  
**Wallet/usage = marketing + utility + auth message charges**  
User ko dashboard mein clearly dikhna chahiye: “Plan ka paisa alag, WhatsApp message spend alag.”

**Phase 1: Pricing Foundation**
Define final product plans and limits.

- Free, Starter, Growth, Pro, Enterprise plans finalize karna.
- Har plan ke limits define karna:
  - WhatsApp numbers
  - contacts
  - agents
  - flows
  - broadcasts/day or month
  - templates
  - AI bot access
  - analytics/reporting
  - integrations/webhooks
- Message charges ko subscription se separate rakhna.
- “Fair use policy” define karna, especially broadcast/automation ke liye.
- Existing `WhatsApp Pro` / `WhatsApp Premium` naming ko new plan model se align karna.

**Phase 2: Database Billing Architecture**
Billing ko production-ready schema dena.

Tables needed:

- `subscription_plans`
- `plan_features`
- `user_subscriptions`
- `message_wallets`
- `wallet_transactions`
- `message_usage_logs`
- `message_rate_cards`
- `invoices` or `billing_events`
- optional: `usage_daily_summaries`

Important fields:

- user/org id
- plan id
- subscription status
- current period start/end
- wallet balance
- message category: `marketing`, `utility`, `authentication`, `service`
- charged amount
- Meta cost
- platform markup, agar future mein lagana ho
- message delivery status
- campaign/broadcast id
- conversation/contact id

**Phase 3: Rate Card System**
Marketing aur utility charge dikhane ke liye dynamic rate card banana hoga.

- India default rates seed karna.
- Categories:
  - Marketing
  - Utility
  - Authentication
  - Service
- Service messages ko ₹0 show karna.
- Rate card admin-editable future ke liye.
- Meta pricing change hone par code deploy ki zaroorat na pade.
- User ko pricing page par line dikhani hai:
  “WhatsApp/Meta message charges are billed separately from your subscription.”

**Phase 4: Wallet / Recharge System**
User pehle wallet recharge karega, phir messages send honge.

- Wallet balance dashboard mein show karna.
- Razorpay payment link/recharge flow banana.
- Recharge plans:
  - ₹500
  - ₹1,000
  - ₹2,500
  - ₹5,000
  - Custom
- Wallet transaction ledger:
  - recharge
  - message debit
  - refund/adjustment
  - failed debit
- Low balance alert:
  - below ₹100
  - below estimated campaign cost
- Broadcast send karne se pehle estimated cost show karna.

**Phase 5: Usage Tracking**
Har outbound paid message ka spend log hoga.

Track this:

- message id
- recipient/contact
- message category
- template name
- campaign id
- rate applied
- charged amount
- delivery status
- sent at / delivered at
- wallet balance after debit

Logic:

- Marketing template delivered/send attempt par charge estimate.
- Utility template charge.
- Service reply within allowed window ₹0.
- Failed messages ka treatment decide karna hoga: ideally delivered billing model ke hisaab se final delivery status par adjust karna.

**Phase 6: User Billing Dashboard**
Yeh tumhari request ka important part hai.

Dashboard mein sections:

- Current plan
- Subscription renewal date
- Wallet balance
- This month message spend
- Today’s spend
- Category-wise spend:
  - Marketing: ₹X
  - Utility: ₹Y
  - Authentication: ₹Z
  - Service: ₹0
- Message count by category
- Campaign-wise spend
- Recent wallet transactions
- Download CSV report
- Low balance warning

Example cards:

- “Wallet Balance: ₹1,240”
- “June Spend: ₹836”
- “Marketing Messages: 780 sent, ₹686 spent”
- “Utility Messages: 1,200 sent, ₹150 spent”
- “Service Replies: 3,400 sent, Free”

**Phase 7: Pricing Page Update**
Current billing UI ko replace/refine karna.

- New plans add karna: Free, Starter, Growth, Pro, Enterprise.
- Monthly/yearly toggle.
- Yearly discount.
- Plan comparison table.
- Separate “WhatsApp Message Charges” section.
- Rate table:
  - Marketing: ₹X/message
  - Utility: ₹Y/message
  - Authentication: ₹Z/message
  - Service: Free
- Clear note:
  “Message charges are deducted from wallet based on usage.”

**Phase 8: Feature Limit Enforcement**
Sirf UI par lock nahi, backend par bhi enforce karna.

Enforce:

- free plan cannot send broadcast
- contact import limit
- max agents
- max flows
- max connected numbers
- campaign scheduler locked by plan
- webhook/API access locked by plan
- wallet balance required before paid campaigns

This prevents revenue leak.

**Phase 9: Broadcast Cost Estimator**
Broadcast page par send se pehle estimate show karna.

Example:

“Recipients: 2,000  
Template category: Marketing  
Estimated cost: ₹1,760  
Wallet balance: ₹2,500  
Remaining after send: ₹740”

If insufficient balance:

“Recharge required: ₹1,020”

**Phase 10: Admin Controls**
Tumhare liye internal admin system.

- Change user plan manually
- Add wallet credit/debit manually
- View user usage
- See high spend users
- See failed payment users
- Update rate card
- Freeze account if abuse/spam risk
- Export billing reports

**Phase 11: Compliance & Risk Guardrails**
WhatsApp automation mein yeh zaroori hai.

- No “unlimited bulk messaging” wording.
- Add unsubscribe/opt-out support.
- Campaign warm-up limits.
- Daily sending limits by plan.
- Spam/failure rate monitoring.
- Template category clarity.
- User ko warning: promotional content marketing category mein charge hoga.
- Official API vs QR/Baileys architecture ka positioning carefully decide karna.

**Phase 12: Subscription Lifecycle**
Production subscription handling.

- Trial
- Active
- Past due
- Cancelled
- Expired
- Grace period
- Auto downgrade to Free
- Renewal reminder
- Payment success/failure webhook
- Invoice record
- Upgrade/downgrade proration later

**Implementation Order Recommended**
1. Database schema for plans, subscriptions, wallet, usage logs.
2. Backend billing service: plan limits + wallet debit + usage logging.
3. Rate card seed.
4. Billing dashboard UI.
5. Pricing page UI.
6. Broadcast cost estimator.
7. Feature limit enforcement.
8. Razorpay recharge flow.
9. Admin controls.
10. Reports/export.

Sabse pehle humein **billing data model** implement karna chahiye. Agar schema solid ban gaya, baaki dashboard, pricing page, wallet, reports sab cleanly build ho jayega.

```
// Map raw plan IDs â†’ display names
function resolvePlanName(plan) {
    if (!plan) return 'Free'
    const p = plan.toLowerCase()
    if (p.includes('all_in_one') || p.includes('ultimate') || p.includes('enterprise')) return 'GAP Ultimate Ecosystem'
    if (p.includes('whatsapp_premium') || p.includes('premium')) return 'WhatsApp Premium'
    if (p.includes('whatsapp_pro') || p.includes('whatsapp')) return 'WhatsApp Pro'
    if (p === 'free' || p === '') return 'Free'
    return plan // keep as-is for known names like "GAP Ultimate Ecosystem"
}
```

```
// POST /api/broadcast/send
app.post('/api/broadcast/header-media', authMiddleware, upload.single('file'), async (req: any, res) => {
    const orgId = req.organization_id;
    const file = req.file;

        if (!orgId) {
```

```
function getPlanName(planId: string): string {
  if (!planId) return "Growth";
  const p = planId.toLowerCase();
  if (p.includes("starter")) return "Starter";
  if (p.includes("growth")) return "Growth";
  if (p === "pro" || p.includes("whatsapp_pro")) return "Pro";
  if (p.includes("premium")) return "Pro";
  if (p.includes("all_in_one") || p.includes("ultimate")) return "GAP Ultimate Ecosystem";
  return "Growth";
}
```

Ab billing hook simple but safe rakha hai: rate card missing ho to fallback rate use hoga, wallet insufficient ho to campaign crash nahi hogi but usage log mein billing_status `failed` rahega. Next phase mein hum send-before-balance blocking add karenge.

```json
{
  "input": "*** Begin Patch\n*** Update File: backend/server.ts\n@@\n const DEFAULT_WHATSAPP_RATE_CARD: Record<string, { category: string; label: string; rate_paise: number; description: string }> = {\n@@\n     }\n };\n+\n+type WhatsappBillingCategory = 'marketing' | 'utility' | 'authentication' | 'service';\n+\n+function normalizeWhatsappBillingCategory(value: any, fallback: WhatsappBillingCategory = 'marketing'): WhatsappBillingCategory {\n+    const raw = String(value || '').toLowerCase().trim();\n+    if (raw.includes('utility')) return 'utility';\n+    if (raw.includes('auth')) return 'authentication';\n+    if (raw.includes('service')) return 'service';\n+    if (raw.includes('marketing')) return 'marketing';\n+    return fallback;\n+}\n+\n+async function getActiveWhatsappRate(category: WhatsappBillingCategory) {\n+    const fallback = DEFAULT_WHATSAPP_RATE_CARD[category] || DEFAULT_WHATSAPP_RATE_CARD.marketing;\n+    try {\n+        const { data, error } = await supabase\n+            .from('whatsapp_rate_cards')\n+            .select('rate_paise, pass_through_rate_paise, markup_paise')\n+            .eq('market', DEFAULT_BILLING_MARKET)\n+            .eq('currency', DEFAULT_BILLING_CURRENCY)\n+            .eq('category', category)\n+            .eq('is_active', true)\n+            .order('effective_from', { ascending: false })\n+            .limit(1)\n+            .maybeSingle();\n+\n+        if (error || !data) {\n+            return {\n+                rate_paise: fallback.rate_paise,\n+                pass_through_rate_paise: fallback.rate_paise,\n+                markup_paise: 0,\n+            };\n+        }\n+        return data;\n+    } catch {\n+        return {\n+            rate_paise: fallback.rate_paise,\n+            pass_through_rate_paise: fallback.rate_paise,\n+            markup_paise: 0,\n+        };\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+async function recordWhatsappMessageUsage(params: {\n+    organization_id: string;\n+    wa_account_id?: string | null;\n+
```

- Database billing SQL applied to Supabase project `uklxlappjcuvdqjvecfh`

  - `create-whatsapp-payment-link` version `23`
  - `verify-whatsapp-subscription` version `24`

- `whatsapp_subscription_plans`: 5 rows
- `whatsapp_rate_cards`: 4 rows
- `whatsapp_wallets`: 23 rows
- Plans live: Free, Starter, Growth, Pro, Enterprise

Note: `supabase db push` migration history mismatch ki wajah se block hua, kyunki remote mein purani migrations local folder mein nahi hain. Maine safe fallback use kiya: single billing SQL direct `supabase db query --linked --file ...` se apply kiya. Schema live hai, but Supabase migration history table mein yeh local migration as “pushed migration” mark nahi hua.

Also checked Supabase changelog: naye tables Data API exposure behavior change ho sakta hai, but yahan grants visible hain and RLS policies active hain. Source: https://supabase.com/changelog?tags=database

Now adding a generic limit checker and wiring it into these create routes. This closes the “plan exists but not enforced” revenue leak.

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>apply_patch</code></summary>

```json
{
  "input": "*** Begin Patch\n*** Update File: backend/server.ts\n@@\n async function buildBroadcastBillingEstimate(params: {\n@@\n     };\n }\n+\n+async function enforcePlanResourceLimit(params: {\n+    organization_id: string;\n+    resource: 'contacts' | 'flows' | 'ai_agents' | 'agents' | 'numbers';\n+    table: string;\n+    countColumn?: string;\n+    filters?: Record<string, any>;\n+    label: string;\n+}) {\n+    const planInfo = await getOrganizationPlanLimits(params.organization_id);\n+    const limit = Number(planInfo.limits?.[params.resource] ?? -1);\n+    if (limit < 0) return { allowed: true, limit, used: 0, plan: planInfo };\n+\n+    let query = supabase\n+        .from(params.table)\n+        .select(params.countColumn || 'id', { count: 'exact', head: true })\n+        .eq('organization_id', params.organization_id);\n+\n+    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(params.filters || {})) {\n+        if (Array.isArray(value)) query = query.in(key, value);\n+        else query = query.eq(key, value);\n+    }\n+\n+    const { count, error } = await query;\n+    if (error) throw error;\n+    const used = Number(count || 0);\n+\n+    if (used >= limit) {\n+        const err: any = new Error(`${params.label} limit reached for ${planInfo.plan_name} plan (${used}/${limit}). Upgrade your plan to add more.`);\n+        err.statusCode = 402;\n+        err.limit = { resource: params.resource, used, limit, plan: planInfo };\n+        throw err;\n+    }\n+\n+    return { allowed: true, limit, used, plan: planInfo };\n+}\n*** End Patch\n"
}
```

- Pricing plans + rate cards database mein add ho gaye
- Wallet system + transactions add ho gaya
- Marketing/Utility/Auth/Service message cost tracking add ho gaya
- Billing dashboard frontend mein ban gaya
- Dashboard par spend/wallet strip add ho gaya
- Broadcast launch se pehle estimated cost + wallet check add ho gaya
- Backend mein plan limits enforce ho rahe hain
- Razorpay plan subscription functions update ho gaye
- Wallet recharge Edge Functions create/deploy ho gaye
- Meta embedded signup URL/config set ho gaya
- Supabase migration live DB par apply ho gayi
- Frontend build aur backend TypeScript check pass ho chuke hain

2. Billing dashboard data sahi aa raha hai ya nahi check karna

4. Razorpay payment/recharge callback real flow test karna

<proposed_plan>
# WhatsApp Service Completion Plan

## Summary
Abhi feature “complete” nahi maana jayega jab tak user ko AiSensy-style productized flow na mile: wallet clearly visible ho, Official Meta Cloud API connect reliable ho, hosted signup fallback card remove ho, aur new business number ke liye assisted request page ho. Final model: **Guided self-serve Meta onboarding + assisted new number request**.

## Key Changes
- **WhatsApp Connect page**
  - “Meta-hosted Embedded Signup” blue fallback card, raw URL, and hosted signup CTA remove karna.
  - Main CTA sirf `Connect with Meta` rahega using official FB Embedded Signup SDK.
  - User-facing copy ko service-style banana: “Connect your business WhatsApp number”, “Prepare business details”, “Verify number by OTP”, “After connect dashboard unlocks”.
  - Technical fields like WABA ID/token ko default user flow se hide/secondary advanced section me rakhna.
  - Connected number ke baad cards show karna: number, WABA ID masked/secondary, send readiness, templates status, wallet balance, next actions.

- **Official Meta Cloud API reliability**
  - `/api/wa/connect/callback` ko harden karna:
    - Meta token exchange errors clearly return kare.
    - WABA and phone discovery fail hone par actionable error.
    - Connected account save ke baad diagnostics auto-run.
  - `/api/whatsapp/accounts` response me `send_ready`, `diagnostics_summary`, and `connection_type: meta_cloud_api | qr_session` add karna.
  - Connect page par “Check Send Access” manual button ke saath auto status refresh bhi rakhna.

- **Wallet visibility**
  - Wallet sirf Billing page par nahi, WhatsApp Connect page aur Dashboard top strip par bhi clearly show hoga.
  - If wallet row missing ho, backend overview endpoint wallet create karke same response me fresh wallet return karega.
  - Empty wallet state: “Recharge before sending campaigns” CTA.
  - Spend cards: Marketing, Utility, Authentication, Service category-wise visible rahenge.

- **New Business Number page**
  - New route: `/whatsapp-number`
  - Sidebar/nav me “New Number” ya “Buy Number” item add karna.
  - Page purpose: user apne business ke liye fresh/dedicated WhatsApp number request kare.
  - Flow:
    - User business name, country, preferred city/state, use case, expected monthly messages, contact email/phone submit kare.
    - App request ko DB me save kare.
    - Status: `requested`, `in_review`, `number_arranged`, `meta_onboarding_pending`, `connected`, `cancelled`.
    - User ko clearly batana: official WhatsApp Cloud API ke liye number OTP/access aur Meta policy approval required hota hai; team assisted setup karegi.
  - New backend APIs:
    - `POST /api/whatsapp/number-requests`
    - `GET /api/whatsapp/number-requests`
  - New Supabase table:
    - `whatsapp_number_requests`
    - org/user ownership, business details, preferred number info, status, admin notes, timestamps.

- **Navigation and UX**
  - WhatsApp setup journey:
    1. Choose existing number connect via Meta
    2. Or request new business number
    3. Recharge wallet
    4. Create templates
    5. Launch campaigns / automate flows
  - QR Session section ko clearly “Testing only” banana, production recommended nahi.
  - Hosted URL env vars/code cleanup only where no longer used by frontend; backend can keep helper unused only if harmless, otherwise remove.

## Test Plan
- Frontend:
  - `npm run build`
  - Verify `/whatsapp-connect`, `/billing`, `/dashboard`, `/whatsapp-number` render without overlap on mobile/tablet/desktop.
  - Connect page par hosted signup card/raw URL absent ho.
  - Wallet balance visible on Billing, Dashboard, and Connect page.
- Backend:
  - `npx tsc --noEmit`
  - Test `/api/billing/overview` returns wallet even when wallet row initially missing.
  - Test number request create/list with authenticated org user.
  - Test `/api/whatsapp/accounts` does not expose encrypted tokens.
- Manual QA:
  - Local backend `localhost:3001` + frontend run karke pages verify.
  - Meta Embedded Signup HTTPS/ngrok/deployed domain se test.
  - Connected account ke baad diagnostics/send-ready state verify.
  - Wallet recharge and broadcast estimate flow verify.

## Assumptions
- New number flow v1 will be **assisted request**, direct in-app telecom inventory/payment sale nahi.
- Official Meta flow will be **guided self-serve**: user Meta admin login/OTP/consent complete karega; platform technical details hide karega and setup guide karega.
- Meta policies/business verification bypass nahi kiya ja sakta; app sirf official process ko simpler banayega.
</proposed_plan>


---

## Test Plan
- Frontend:
  - `npm run build`
  - Verify `/whatsapp-connect`, `/billing`, `/dashboard`, `/whatsapp-number` render without overlap on mobile/tablet/desktop.
  - Connect page par hosted signup card/raw URL absent ho.
  - Wallet balance visible on Billing, Dashboard, and Connect page.
- Backend:
  - `npx tsc --noEmit`
  - Test `/api/billing/overview` returns wallet even when wallet row initially missing.
  - Test number request create/list with authenticated org user.
  - Test `/api/whatsapp/accounts` does not expose encrypted tokens.
- Manual QA:
  - Local backend `localhost:3001` + frontend run karke pages verify.
  - Meta Embedded Signup HTTPS/ngrok/deployed domain se test.
  - Connected account ke baad diagnostics/send-ready state verify.
  - Wallet recharge and broadcast estimate flow verify.

## Assumptions
- New number flow v1 will be **assisted request**, direct in-app telecom inventory/payment sale nahi.
- Official Meta flow will be **guided self-serve**: user Meta admin login/OTP/consent complete karega; platform technical details hide karega and setup guide karega.
- Meta policies/business verification bypass nahi kiya ja sakta; app sirf official process ko simpler banayega.

# Context from my IDE setup:

## Active file: supabase/migrations/20260609113113_whatsapp_number_requests.sql

## Active selection of the file:
-- Assisted new WhatsApp business number requests.
-- Users request a fresh/dedicated number; the operations team handles sourcing and official Meta onboarding support.

create table if not exists public.whatsapp_number_requests (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  organization_id uuid not null references public.organizations(id) on delete cascade,
  user_id uuid references auth.users(id) on delete set null,
  business_name text not null,
  country text not null default 'India',
  preferred_region text,
  use_case text not null,
  expected_monthly_messages integer check (expected_monthly_messages is null or expected_monthly_messages >= 0),
  contact_name text,
  contact_email text,
  contact_phone text,
  status text not null default 'requested'
    check (status in ('requested', 'in_review', 'number_arranged', 'meta_onboarding_pending', 'connected', 'cancelled')),
  admin_notes text,
  metadata jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now()
);

create index if not exists idx_whatsapp_number_requests_org_created
  on public.whatsapp_number_requests(organization_id, created_at desc);

create index if not exists idx_whatsapp_number_requests_status
  on public.whatsapp_number_requests(status, created_at desc);

alter table public.whatsapp_number_requests enable row level security;

drop policy if exists "Org members can read own whatsapp number requests" on public.whatsapp_number_requests;
create policy "Org members can read own whatsapp number requests"
  on public.whatsapp_number_requests for select
  using (
    exists (
      select 1 from public.organization_members om
      where om.organization_id = whatsapp_number_requests.organization_id
        and om.user_id = auth.uid()
        and coalesce(om.is_active, true) = true
    )
  );

grant select, insert, update on public.whatsapp_number_requests to authenticated;

Haan, `Connect with Meta` button **actual official Meta Embedded Signup flow start karta hai**, but connection tabhi complete hota hai jab:

1. Meta popup open ho
2. User Meta admin login kare
3. WABA select/create kare
4. Phone number add/verify OTP kare
5. Meta frontend ko `code` return kare
6. Backend `/api/wa/connect/callback` us code ko token me exchange karke WABA/phone save kare

Uske baad number `Connected numbers` section me show hona chahiye.

Screenshot wala error **Connect with Meta ka nahi lag raha**. Ye Billing page ke wallet recharge button se aa raha hai:

`Edge Function returned a non-2xx status code`

Matlab Supabase Edge Function `create-whatsapp-wallet-recharge-link` fail ho rahi hai, likely Razorpay env/config issue. Connect with Meta backend route Edge Function use nahi karta.

Ek aur important cheez: tumhare `frontend/.env` me `VITE_BACKEND_URL` do baar hai. Last wala active hota hai:

```env
VITE_BACKEND_URL=https://parted-deuce-penpal.ngrok-free.dev
```

Toh localhost frontend actually backend localhost nahi, ngrok backend call kar raha hai. Agar local backend test karna hai toh sirf ye rakho:

```env
VITE_BACKEND_URL=http://localhost:3001
```

Phir frontend restart karo.

Meta testing ke liye best:
- frontend/backend dono HTTPS/ngrok ya deployed domain par test karo
- Meta app settings me domain/redirect URL allow ho
- backend `.env` ka `META_REDIRECT_URI` same public URL se match kare

Short answer: **button real official connect flow hai**, lekin user ko Meta verification/OTP complete karna hi padega. Screenshot ka error wallet recharge Edge Function ka hai, WhatsApp connect ka nahi.

```
import { createClient } from "https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js@2";

const RAZORPAY_KEY_ID = Deno.env.get("RAZORPAY_KEY_ID");
```

Issue ka exact reason mil gaya: **Supabase Edge Function chal rahi hai, but Razorpay credentials invalid/mismatched hain.** Direct test me response aaya:

```json
{"success":false,"error":"Authentication failed"}
```

Maine code-side fix kar diya:
- Wallet recharge + verify functions now `RAZORPAY_LIVE_*`, `RAZORPAY_TEST_*`, aur default `RAZORPAY_KEY_*` sab try karte hain.
- Plan payment functions bhi same fix ke saath redeploy ho gaye.
- Billing page ab generic `non-2xx` ke bajay actual error show karega.
- Frontend build pass hai.

Ab tumhe Razorpay dashboard se **valid key pair** set karna hai:

```powershell
npx supabase secrets set RAZORPAY_LIVE_KEY_ID=rzp_live_xxxxx RAZORPAY_LIVE_KEY_SECRET=your_live_secret
```

Ya testing ke liye:

```powershell
npx supabase secrets set RAZORPAY_TEST_KEY_ID=rzp_test_xxxxx RAZORPAY_TEST_KEY_SECRET=your_test_secret
```

Important: `KEY_ID` aur `KEY_SECRET` **same Razorpay account aur same mode** ke hone chahiye. Live ID + test secret mix hua toh same `Authentication failed` aayega.

Set karne ke baad `/billing` par ₹500 recharge click karke test karo. Vite dev server chal raha hai toh page refresh kar lena; frontend patch ke baad alert me actual Razorpay error dikhega.

Fix ho gaya. Maine test Razorpay mode setup kar diya:

- Supabase secrets me `RAZORPAY_MODE=test` set ho gaya.
- `RAZORPAY_TEST_KEY_ID` aur `RAZORPAY_TEST_KEY_SECRET` set ho gaye.
- Edge Functions update/deploy ho gaye so live secrets saved reh sakte hain, but abhi testing me test keys priority lenge.
- Direct function test successful hai: payment link create ho gaya.
- Frontend build pass hai.

Ab `/billing` page refresh karo aur ₹500 recharge click karo. Ab test Razorpay payment link open hona chahiye.

Mode switch karna ho toh:

```powershell
npx supabase secrets set RAZORPAY_MODE=live
```

Testing par wapas:

```powershell
npx supabase secrets set RAZORPAY_MODE=test
```

Aur haan, `VITE_RAZORPAY_KEY_SECRET` frontend `.env` me kabhi mat rakhna. Secret sirf Supabase Edge Function secrets me rehna chahiye.

What happened:
- Payment link test Razorpay account me tha.
- Verify function wrong/default Razorpay key se fetch kar raha tha, isliye `The id provided does not exist` aa raha tha.
- Maine default `RAZORPAY_KEY_ID/SECRET` ko bhi test pair pe set kiya, while live keys `RAZORPAY_LIVE_*` me saved rehengi.
- Verify function redeploy kiya.
- Same paid link verify karke confirm kiya.

Confirmed DB result:
- `status`: `completed`
- `balance_paise`: `50000`
- Wallet credited: ₹500

Ab page refresh karo ya `/billing` par jao, wallet ₹500 show hona chahiye. Future me live mode karna ho toh:

```powershell
npx supabase secrets set RAZORPAY_MODE=live RAZORPAY_KEY_ID=rzp_live_xxx RAZORPAY_KEY_SECRET=live_secret
```

Testing mode ke liye current setup ready hai.
